## Instruction

There is a class schedule for the first semester of the 2025-26 academic year in the workspace. I want to take Natural Language Processing (Ëá™ÁÑ∂ËØ≠Ë®ÄÂ§ÑÁêÜ) and Software Architecture (ËΩØ‰ª∂‰ΩìÁ≥ªÁªìÊûÑ). In addition, I want to take one Ideological and Political Theory (B categoryÔºåÊÄùÊîøB) class on Monday and one General Education Core Curriculum class (ÈÄöËØÜÊïôËÇ≤Ê†∏ÂøÉËØæÁ®ã) on Monday, and I hope that both of these have open-book exams instead of other forms of assessment. Please help me find these courses and output the results according to the format in reference_format.xlsx in the workspace. If there are multiple options for course selection, please save each option in a separate Excel file. To keep the workspace clean, please only keep the .xlsx files of each course selection scheme in the end, and delete any other unnecessary Excel files (including the reference format). The final .xlsx files should contain values in Chinese, but retain the original English headers.

```python 
# Let's create a function to help organize the course data
def create_course_data(courses):
    """
    Convert course list to Excel data format
    Headers: Course name, Course ID, Instructor, Campus, Class Time, Enrollment, Credits, Assessment Method, Exam Time, Course Selection Restrictions
    """
    headers = ["Course name", "Course ID", "Instructor", "Campus", "Class Time", "Enrollment", "Credits", "Assessment Method", "Exam Time", "Course Selection Restrictions"]
    data = [headers]
    
    for course in courses:
        data.append([
            course.get('name', ''),
            course.get('id', ''),
            course.get('instructor', ''),
            course.get('campus', ''),
            course.get('time', ''),
            course.get('enrollment', ''),
            course.get('credits', ''),
            course.get('assessment', ''),
            course.get('exam_time', ''),
            course.get('restrictions', '')
        ])
    
    return data

# Define the courses we found
```

```python 
# Let's create a function to help organize the course data
def create_course_data(courses):
    """
    Convert course list to Excel data format
    Headers: Course name, Course ID, Instructor, Campus, Class Time, Enrollment, Credits, Assessment Method, Exam Time, Course Selection Restrictions
    """
    headers = ["Course name", "Course ID", "Instructor", "Campus", "Class Time", "Enrollment", "Credits", "Assessment Method", "Exam Time", "Course Selection Restrictions"]
    data = [headers]
    
    for course in courses:
        data.append([
            course.get('name', ''),
            course.get('id', ''),
            course.get('instructor', ''),
            course.get('campus', ''),
            course.get('time', ''),
            course.get('enrollment', ''),
            course.get('credits', ''),
            course.get('assessment', ''),
            course.get('exam_time', ''),
            course.get('restrictions', '')
        ])
    
    return data

# Define the courses we found
```

```python 
# Let's create a function to help organize the course data
def create_course_data(courses):
    """
    Convert course list to Excel data format
    Headers: Course name, Course ID, Instructor, Campus, Class Time, Enrollment, Credits, Assessment Method, Exam Time, Course Selection Restrictions
    """
    headers = ["Course name", "Course ID", "Instructor", "Campus", "Class Time", "Enrollment", "Credits", "Assessment Method", "Exam Time", "Course Selection Restrictions"]
    data = [headers]
    
    for course in courses:
        data.append([
            course.get('name', ''),
            course.get('id', ''),
            course.get('instructor', ''),
            course.get('campus', ''),
            course.get('time', ''),
            course.get('enrollment', ''),
            course.get('credits', ''),
            course.get('assessment', ''),
            course.get('exam_time', ''),
            course.get('restrictions', '')
        ])
    
    return data

# Define the courses we found
```

```json
{
```
